###################
List of Observables
###################


The following is a list of observables that is available in EOS v1.0.10.


*****************************************************
Observables in (semi)leptonic :math:`b`-hadron decays
*****************************************************

Observables in :math:`B^-\to \ell^-\bar\nu` decays
==================================================

.. list-table::
   :widths: 50, 25, 25
   :header-rows: 1

   * - Qualified Name
     - Description
     - Kinematic Variables

       .. _bunummtolnucocobr:
   * - ``B_u->lnu::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - 


The option "l" selects the charged lepton flavor.

Observables in :math:`B^-\to \ell^-\bar\nu\ell'^+\ell'^-` decays
================================================================

.. list-table::
   :widths: 50, 25, 25
   :header-rows: 1

   * - Qualified Name
     - Description
     - Kinematic Variables

       .. _bunummtoenumumucocoaunfb:
   * - ``B_u->enumumu::A_FB``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B^- \to e^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtoenumumucocobr:
   * - ``B_u->enumumu::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to e^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtoenumumucocod2brsldq2sldk2:
   * - ``B_u->enumumu::d2BR/dq2/dk2``
     - :math:`\frac{d\mathcal{B}(B^- \to e^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)}{dq^2/dk^2}`
     - ``q2``, ``k2``

       .. _bunummtomunueecocoaunfb:
   * - ``B_u->munuee::A_FB``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B^- \to \mu^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtomunueecocobr:
   * - ``B_u->munuee::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \mu^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtomunueecocod2brsldq2sldk2:
   * - ``B_u->munuee::d2BR/dq2/dk2``
     - :math:`\frac{d\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \mu^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)}{dq^2/dk^2}`
     - ``q2``, ``k2``

       .. _bunummtotaunueecocoaunfb:
   * - ``B_u->taunuee::A_FB``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtotaunueecocobr:
   * - ``B_u->taunuee::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtotaunueecocod2brsldq2sldk2:
   * - ``B_u->taunuee::d2BR/dq2/dk2``
     - :math:`\frac{d\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu e^+e^-)}{dq^2/dk^2}`
     - ``q2``, ``k2``

       .. _bunummtotaunumumucocoaunfb:
   * - ``B_u->taunumumu::A_FB``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtotaunumumucocobr:
   * - ``B_u->taunumumu::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``, ``k2_min``, ``k2_max``

       .. _bunummtotaunumumucocod2brsldq2sldk2:
   * - ``B_u->taunumumu::d2BR/dq2/dk2``
     - :math:`\frac{d\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \tau^-\bar\nu\mu^+\mu^-)}{dq^2/dk^2}`
     - ``q2``, ``k2``


The option "l" selects the charged lepton flavour coming out of the weak current, "lprime" selects the lepton flavour coming out of the photon.

Observables in :math:`B\to \pi \ell^-\bar\nu` decays
====================================================

.. list-table::
   :widths: 50, 25, 25
   :header-rows: 1

   * - Qualified Name
     - Description
     - Kinematic Variables

       .. _bmmtopilnucocoaunfb:
   * - ``B->pilnu::A_FB``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B\to \pi\ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocoaunfbpoq2pc:
   * - ``B->pilnu::A_FB(q2)``
     - :math:`A_{\mathrm{FB}}(B\to \pi\ell^-\bar\nu)(q^2)`
     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocoaunl:
   * - ``B->pilnu::A_l``
     - n/a
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocobr:
   * - ``B->pilnu::BR``
     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocofunh:
   * - ``B->pilnu::F_H``
     - n/a
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocoppoq2pc:
   * - ``B->pilnu::P(q2)``
     - :math:`dP(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)/dq^2\, \left[ \textrm{GeV}^{-2} \right]`
     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocoppoq2unmin,q2unmaxpc:
   * - ``B->pilnu::P(q2_min,q2_max)``
     - :math:`P(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocorunpi:
   * - ``B->pilnu::R_pi``
     - :math:`R_{\pi}`
     - ``q2_mu_max``, ``q2_mu_min``, ``q2_tau_max``, ``q2_tau_min``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocorunpipoq2pc:
   * - ``B->pilnu::R_pi(q2)``
     - :math:`R_{\pi}(q^2)`
     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocorunpiun0:
   * - ``B->pilnu::R_pi_0``
     - :math:`R_{\pi, 0}`
     - ``q2_mu_max``, ``q2_mu_min``, ``q2_tau_max``, ``q2_tau_min``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocorunpiunp:
   * - ``B->pilnu::R_pi_p``
     - :math:`R_{\pi, P}`
     - ``q2_mu_max``, ``q2_mu_min``, ``q2_tau_max``, ``q2_tau_min``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocodbrsldq2:
   * - ``B->pilnu::dBR/dq2``
     - :math:`d\mathcal{B}(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)/dq^2\, \left[ \textrm{GeV}^{-2} \right]`
     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocodca2brsldq2sldcospothetaunlpc:
   * - ``B->pilnu::d^2BR/dq2/dcos(theta_l)``
     - :math:`d^2\mathcal{B}(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)/dq^2/d\cos(\theta_l)\, \left[ \textrm{GeV}^{-2} \right]`
     - ``q2``, ``cos(theta_l)``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocowidth:
   * - ``B->pilnu::width``
     - :math:`\Gamma(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocowidthun0:
   * - ``B->pilnu::width_0``
     - :math:`\Gamma(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)_0`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocowidthunp:
   * - ``B->pilnu::width_p``
     - :math:`\Gamma(B\to\pi\ell^-\bar\nu)_p`
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtopilnucocozeta:
   * - ``B->pilnu::zeta``
     - n/a
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``


The option "l" selects the charged lepton flavor. The option "q" selects the spectator quark flavor. The option "form-factors" selects the form factor parametrization.

     - n/a

     - :math:`R_D`

     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtodlnucocodbrsldq2:
   * - ``B->Dlnu::dBR/dq2``
     - :math:`d\mathcal{B}(B\to \bar{D}\ell^-\bar\nu)/dq^2\, \left[ \textrm{GeV}^{-2} \right]`
     - ``q2``

       .. _bmmtodlnucocodca2brsldq2sldcospothetaunlpc:
   * - ``B->Dlnu::d^2BR/dq2/dcos(theta_l)``
     - :math:`d^2\mathcal{B}(B\to \bar{D}\ell^-\bar\nu)/dq^2/d\cos(\theta_l)\, \left[ \textrm{GeV}^{-2} \right]`
     - ``q2``, ``cos(theta_l)``

       .. _bmmtodlnucoconormbr:
   * - ``B->Dlnu::normBR``
     - n/a
     - ``q2_min``, ``q2_max``

       .. _bmmtodlnucoconormdbrslds:
   * - ``B->Dlnu::normdBR/ds``
     - n/a
     - ``q2``


The option "l" selects the charged lepton flavor. The option "q" selects the spectator quark flavor. The option "form-factors" selects the form factor parametrization.

The option "l" selects the charged lepton flavor. The option "q" selects the spectator quark flavor. The option "form-factors" selects the form factor parametrization.

     - :math:`\mathcal{B}(B^- \to \gamma \ell^-\bar\nu)`
     - ``E_gamma_min``
